add_namespace = poland


#технический ивент на удаление "Польского вопроса"
country_event = {
	id = poland.0
	trigger = {
		tag = POL
		has_variable = POL.polish_question_GER_influence
		OR = {
			NOT = { is_subject_of = GER is_subject_of = AUH }
			GER = { has_war_with = AUH }
			has_global_flag = WWI_AUH_HAS_CAPITULATED
			has_global_flag = WWI_GER_HAS_CAPITULATED
		}
	}
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }
	immediate = {
		GER = { clr_country_flag = polish_question_des_cat_flag }
		AUH = { clr_country_flag = polish_question_des_cat_flag }
		clear_variable = POL.polish_question_GER_influence
		clear_variable = POL.polish_question_AUH_influence
	}
}

#Польское обращение (не Польская просьба)
country_event = {
	id = poland.1
	title = poland.1.t
	desc = {
		text = poland.1.desc
		trigger = { tag = GER }
	}
	desc = {
		text = poland.1.desc_1
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = GER } }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_pol_prosb_k_ger
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = polish_question_territory_formal_trasnfer } }
		name = poland.1.a #Отказать
		set_country_flag = polish_question_territory_formal_trasnfer_ban
		if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			POL = { country_event = { id = poland.2 hours = 6 } }
			else = {
				POL = { country_event = { id = poland.2 hours = 9 } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = AUH
				NOT = { has_country_flag = polish_question_territory_formal_trasnfer_ban }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = polish_question_territory_formal_trasnfer_ban } }
		name = poland.1.b #Согласиться на формальную передачу
		set_country_flag = polish_question_territory_formal_trasnfer
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = POL modifier = BLR_Ylychenie_otnocheniy }
		if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			hidden_effect = {
				add_to_variable = { POL.polish_question_GER_influence = 3 }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { POL.polish_question_GER_influence > 10 } }
					set_variable = { POL.polish_question_GER_influence = 10 }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = polish_question_GER_influence_plus_3
			POL = { country_event = { id = poland.3 hours = 6 } }
			AUH = { country_event = { id = poland.4 hours = 12 } }
			else = {
				hidden_effect = {
					add_to_variable = { POL.polish_question_AUH_influence = 3 }
					if = {
						limit = { check_variable = { POL.polish_question_AUH_influence > 10 } }
						set_variable = { POL.polish_question_AUH_influence = 10 }
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = polish_question_AUH_influence_plus_3
				POL = { country_event = { id = poland.3 hours = 9 } }
				GER = { country_event = { id = poland.4 hours = 15 } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = GER
				has_opinion = { target = POL value < 0 }
			}
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 9 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 19 } }
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 29 } }
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 49 } }
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 69 } }
			modifier = { factor = 4 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 79 } }
			modifier = { factor = 4 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 89 } }
			modifier = { factor = 4 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 99 } }
		}
	}
}

#Вмешательство в польские дела
country_event = {
	id = poland.4
	title = poland.4.t
	desc = {
		text = poland.4.desc
		trigger = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = poland.4.desc_1
		trigger = { FROM = { NOT = { tag = GER } } }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_pol_prosb_k_ger
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = polish_question_territory_formal_trasnfer } }
		name = poland.4.a #Они совершают ошибку
		set_country_flag = polish_question_territory_formal_trasnfer_ban
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = POL modifier = GER_AUH_POL_dispute }
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = GER_AUH_POL_dispute }
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = FROM modifier = GER_AUH_POL_dispute }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = AUH
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = polish_question_territory_formal_trasnfer_ban } }
		name = poland.4.b #Их жест можно приветствовать
		set_country_flag = polish_question_territory_formal_trasnfer
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = GER
				has_opinion = { target = POL value < 0 }
			}
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 9 } }
			modifier = { factor = 2 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 19 } }
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 29 } }
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 49 } }
			modifier = { factor = 3 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 69 } }
			modifier = { factor = 4 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 79 } }
			modifier = { factor = 4 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 89 } }
			modifier = { factor = 4 has_opinion = { target = POL value > 99 } }
		}
	}
}

#Перераспределение полномочий в Польше
country_event = {
	id = poland.5
	title = poland.5.t
	desc = poland.5.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_pol_prosb_k_ger
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = AUH }
				GER = {
					if = {
						limit = { controls_state = 1120 controls_state = 1166 controls_state = 1116 }
						if = {
							limit = { has_war_with = RUS }
							RUS = { set_state_owner = 10 }
						}
						if = {
							limit = { 10 = { CONTROLLER = { NOT = { tag = GER has_war_with = GER } } } }
							set_state_controller = 10
						}
					}
				}
				AUH = { POL = { subject_owner_change_script = yes } }
				subtract_from_variable = { POL.polish_question_GER_influence = 5 }
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { POL.polish_question_GER_influence < 0 } }
					set_variable = { POL.polish_question_GER_influence = 0 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.5.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			GER = { end_puppet = POL }
			AUH = { puppet = POL }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = polish_question_GER_influence_minus_5
		if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUH modifier = GER_AUH_POL_stealing }
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = POL NOT = { is_core_of = GER } }
				add_compliance = -50
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = LIT tag = UKR } is_subject_of = GER }
				add_autonomy_score = {
					value = 200
					localization = poland_5_autonomy_tt
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = AUH }
			effect_tooltip = {
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = GER modifier = GER_AUH_POL_stealing }
				POL = {
					add_autonomy_score = {
						value = 300
						localization = poland_5_autonomy_tt
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = POL }
			add_autonomy_score = {
				value = 300
				localization = poland_5_autonomy_tt
			}
		}
	}
}

#Австро-польское требование
country_event = {
	id = poland.6
	title = poland.6.t
	desc = poland.6.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_pol_prosb_k_ger
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.6.a #Пусть сами разбираются в этом дерьме
		remove_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AUH
			modifier = GER_AUH_POL_stealing
		}
		remove_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AUH
			modifier = GER_AUH_POL_dispute
		}
		AUH = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = GER
				modifier = GER_AUH_POL_dispute
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = POL
				OR = {
					region = 38
					state = 92
				}
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT state = 1001 state = 1119 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_owned_by = GER }
				set_state_owner_to = POL
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_controlled_by = GER }
				set_state_controller_to = POL
			}
		}
		AUH = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER } }
				create_faction_from_template = {
					template = faction_template_european_dominance_monarchist
					name = AUS_Viena_pact
					icon = GFX_faction_logo_generic_2
					color = { 100 100 150 }
				}
				POL = {
					if = {
						limit = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
						leave_faction = yes
					}
				}
				add_to_faction = POL
			}
		}
		POL = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUH modifier = GER_AUH_POL_AUH_support } }
		GER = { clr_country_flag = polish_question_des_cat_flag }
		AUH = { clr_country_flag = polish_question_des_cat_flag }
		clear_variable = POL.polish_question_GER_influence
		clear_variable = POL.polish_question_AUH_influence
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.6.b #Этому не бывать
		POL = {
			create_wargoal = {
				type = take_state_focus
				target = GER
				generator = { 10 1166 87 1115 1117 98 1120 1118 1116 1120 90 92 }
				expire = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = WWI_is_now } }
			AUH = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
					leave_faction = yes
				}
			}
			POL = {
				if = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
					leave_faction = yes
				}
			}
			AUH = {
				create_faction_from_template = {
					template = faction_template_european_dominance_monarchist
					name = AUS_Viena_pact
					icon = GFX_faction_logo_generic_2
					color = { 100 100 150 }
				}
				add_to_faction = POL
			}
		}
		POL = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = AUH modifier = GER_AUH_POL_AUH_support } }
		GER = { clr_country_flag = polish_question_des_cat_flag }
		AUH = { clr_country_flag = polish_question_des_cat_flag }
		clear_variable = POL.polish_question_GER_influence
		clear_variable = POL.polish_question_AUH_influence
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

#Разгон правительства
country_event = {
	id = poland.7
	title = poland.7.t
	desc = {
		text = poland.7.desc
		trigger = { is_subject_of = GER }
	}
	desc = {
		text = poland.7.desc_1
		trigger = { NOT = { is_subject_of = GER } }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_pol_prosb_k_ger
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.7.a #Мы сделали всё что можно
		GER = { clr_country_flag = polish_question_des_cat_flag }
		AUH = { clr_country_flag = polish_question_des_cat_flag }
		clear_variable = POL.polish_question_GER_influence
		clear_variable = POL.polish_question_AUH_influence
		if = {
			limit = { OVERLORD = { has_war_with = RUS } }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { NOT = { state = 1466 state = 1467 state = 925 state = 88 is_core_of = GAL } }
				set_state_owner_to = RUS
			}
		}
		OVERLORD = {
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				change_tag_from = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}




country_event = {
	id = poland.11
	title = poland.11.t
	desc = poland.11.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_greece_civil_war_soldiers
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.11.a
		FROM = { country_event = poland.17 }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = { add = 100 surrender_progress < 0.10 }
			modifier = { add = 5 war_length_with = { tag = POL months < 12 } }
			modifier = { add = 5 war_length_with = { tag = RUS months < 12 } }
			modifier = { add = 2 has_army_manpower = { size > 199999 } }
			modifier = { add = 3 has_army_manpower = { size > 299999 } }
			modifier = { add = 4 has_army_manpower = { size > 399999 } }
			modifier = { add = 5 has_army_manpower = { size > 499999 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = { ROOT = { original_tag = POL } }
		name = poland.11.b
		set_global_flag = POL_RUS_peace_fired
		POL = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = POL_form_army_balahovich
					has_completed_focus = POL_support_rusk_form_pol
					has_country_flag = POL_form_russ_three_army
				}
				activate_mission = POL_bulak_nachinaet_pohod
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_form_army_balahovich }
					has_completed_focus = POL_support_rusk_form_pol
					has_country_flag = POL_form_russ_three_army
				}
				activate_mission = POL_rpk_nachinaet_pohod
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OVERLORD = { OR = { tag = FROM tag = ROOT } }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						original_tag = BLR
						NOT = {
							206 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = LIT
						NOT = {
							11 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = LAT
						NOT = {
							12 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = EST
						NOT = {
							812 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						former_russian_empire_ukraine_country = yes
						NOT = {
							202 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
							221 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
							192 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
							227 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
							196 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			OVERLORD = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				OR = {
					original_tag = BLR
					original_tag = UKR
					original_tag = COU
					original_tag = LIT
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = { OWNER = { OR = { tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } CONTROLLER = { OR = { tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } }
					OR = {
						is_core_of = PREV
						is_claimed_by = PREV
					}
				}
				PREV = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OVERLORD = { OR = { tag = FROM tag = ROOT } }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						original_tag = BLR
						NOT = {
							206 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = LIT
						NOT = {
							11 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = LAT
						NOT = {
							12 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = EST
						NOT = {
							812 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						former_russian_empire_ukraine_country = yes
						NOT = {
							202 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
							221 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
							192 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
							227 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
							196 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			OVERLORD = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = { tag = BLR BLR = { is_in_faction_with = POL } country_exists = BLR }
				OR = {
				state = 1443
				state = 1437
				state = 194
				state = 922
				state = 94
				state = 955
				state = 241
				}
			}
			BLR = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { LIT = { has_war_with = FROM } }
			every_country = {
				limit = { OR = { tag = FROM is_in_faction_with = FROM } }
				white_peace = LIT
				remove_wargoal = {
					type = all
					target = LIT
				}
				LIT = {
					remove_wargoal = {
						type = all
						target = PREV

				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_form_army_balahovich }
					has_completed_focus = POL_support_rusk_form_pol
					has_country_flag = POL_form_russ_three_army
				}
				activate_mission = POL_rpk_nachinaet_pohod
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = POL_RUS_peace_fired
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				OR = {
					original_tag = BLR
					original_tag = UKR
					original_tag = COU
					original_tag = LIT
					original_tag = LAT
					original_tag = EST
					original_tag = CRI
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = { OWNER = { OR = { tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } CONTROLLER = { OR = { tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM } } }
					OR = {
						is_core_of = PREV
						is_claimed_by = PREV
					}
				}
				PREV = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OVERLORD = { OR = { tag = ROOT tag = FROM } }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						original_tag = BLR
						NOT = {
							206 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = LIT
						NOT = {
							11 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = LAT
						NOT = {
							12 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = EST
						NOT = {
							812 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						former_russian_empire_ukraine_country = yes
						NOT = {
							202 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } } }
							221 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } } }
							192 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } } }
							227 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } } }
							196 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = FROM is_subject_of = FROM tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			OVERLORD = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = { tag = BLR country_exists = BLR }
				OR = {
				state = 1443
				state = 1437
				state = 194
				state = 922
				state = 94
				state = 955
				state = 241
				state = 204
				}

			BLR = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

			limit = {
				is_owned_by = FROM
				NOT = { is_core_of = FROM }
			}
			ROOT = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = FROM
				OR = { OWNER = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } CONTROLLER = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
			}
			FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

				is_subject_of = FROM
				OR = {
					original_tag = BLR
					original_tag = UKR
					original_tag = COU
					original_tag = LIT
					original_tag = LAT
					original_tag = EST
					original_tag = CRI
				}

				limit = {
					is_core_of = FROM
				}
				FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			FROM = { end_puppet = PREV }
		}
		POL = { dismantle_faction = yes }

			limit = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_in_faction_with = ROOT } }
			FROM = { THIS_white_peace_PREV_buffer = yes }

				type = all
				target = FROM
			}
			FROM = {

					type = all
					target = PREV
				}

		ai_chance = {

			modifier = { add = 3 904 = { OR = { OWNER = { OR = { tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } CONTROLLER = { OR = { tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } } } }
			modifier = { add = 3 war_length_with = { tag = POL months > 12 } }
			modifier = { add = 3 war_length_with = { tag = RUS months > 12 } }

# Польша потерпела поражение от России
country_event = {
	id = poland.14
	title = poland.14.t
	desc = poland.14.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_greece_civil_war_soldiers
	
	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		has_war_with = POL
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		has_government = communism
		RUS = { is_subject = no }
		POL = { is_subject = no }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = POL_RUS_peace_fired }
		POL = {
			surrender_progress > 0.8
			NOT = {
				controls_state = 10
			}
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.14.a
		set_global_flag = POL_RUS_peace_fired
		POL = { 
			clr_country_flag = POL_form_russ_three_army 
			hidden_effect = { 
				remove_mission = POL_rpk_form_cav_divizion2
				remove_mission = POL_rpk_form_divizion2
				remove_mission = POL_rpk_form_cav_divizion
				remove_mission =POL_rpk_form_divizion
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = RUS
				OR = {
					original_tag = BLR
					original_tag = UKR
					original_tag = COU
					original_tag = LIT
					original_tag = LAT
					original_tag = EST
					original_tag = CRI
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OWNER = {
						OR = {
							tag = POL
							is_subject_of = POL
						}
					}
					OR = {
						is_core_of = PREV
						is_claimed_by = PREV
					}
				}
				PREV = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OVERLORD = { OR = { tag = RUS tag = POL } }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						original_tag = BLR
						NOT = {
							206 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = POL is_subject_of = POL tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = LIT
						NOT = {
							11 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = POL is_subject_of = POL tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = LAT
						NOT = {
							12 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = POL is_subject_of = POL tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = EST
						NOT = {
							812 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = POL is_subject_of = POL tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						former_russian_empire_ukraine_country = yes
						NOT = {
							202 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = POL is_subject_of = POL tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } } }
							221 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = POL is_subject_of = POL tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } } }
							192 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = POL is_subject_of = POL tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } } }
							227 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = POL is_subject_of = POL tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } } }
							196 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = POL is_subject_of = POL tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			OVERLORD = {
				annex_country = {
					target = PREV
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = POL
				NOT = { is_core_of = POL }
			}
			RUS = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = RUS
				is_core_of = POL
			}
			POL = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { OR = { tag = RUS is_in_faction_with = RUS } }
			POL = { THIS_white_peace_PREV_buffer = yes }
			remove_wargoal = {
				type = all
				target = POL
			}
			POL = {
				remove_wargoal = {
					type = all
					target = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { RUS = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
			RUS = { add_to_faction = POL }
		}
		POL = {
			add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.15 }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			add_ideas = {
				military_dictatorship_gov_form
				local_assembly_decisions_b_law
				unitary_gov_terr
				allow_one_party_law
				ideological_expansion_law
				workers_control_law
				
				civilian_economy
				disarmed_nation
			}
			create_country_leader = { name = "Jozef Unszlicht" desc = "" picture = "gfx/leaders/SOV/Portrait_Jozef_Unszlicht.dds" ideology = leninism traits = { } }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_subject_of = POL }
			POL = { end_puppet = PREV }
		}
		RUS = { POL = { subjecting_script_with_transfer_parties_dominion = yes } }
	}
}

# Россия потерпела поражение от Польши
country_event = {
	id = poland.15
	title = poland.15.t
	desc = poland.15.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_greece_civil_war_soldiers
	
	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		has_war_with = POL
		has_country_flag = RUS_Oktober_revolution_fired
		has_government = communism
		RUS = { is_subject = no }
		POL = { is_subject = no }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = POL_RUS_peace_fired }
		RUS = {
			surrender_progress > 0.6
			NOT = {
				controls_state = 206
				controls_state = 202
				OR = {
					controls_state = 195
					controls_state = 219
					controls_state = 920
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = poland.15.a
		set_global_flag = POL_RUS_peace_fired
		POL = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = POL_form_army_balahovich
					has_completed_focus = POL_support_rusk_form_pol
					has_country_flag = POL_form_russ_three_army
				}
				activate_mission = POL_bulak_nachinaet_pohod
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_form_army_balahovich }
					has_completed_focus = POL_support_rusk_form_pol
					has_country_flag = POL_form_russ_three_army
				}
				activate_mission = POL_rpk_nachinaet_pohod
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {

					original_tag = BLR

					original_tag = LIT

			}

					AND = {

						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = LIT
						NOT = {
							11 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = POL is_subject_of = POL tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = LAT
						NOT = {
							12 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = POL is_subject_of = POL tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } } }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						original_tag = EST
						NOT = {
							812 = { OR = { OWNER = { tag = PREV.PREV } CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = PREV.PREV NOT = { tag = POL is_subject_of = POL tag = RUS is_subject_of = RUS } } } }
						}
					}

	id = poland.22

	desc = poland.22.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_pol_WGS
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.22.a
		add_ideas = POL_WGR
		add_ideas = Jozef_Mikulowski-Pomorski
		custom_effect_tooltip = POL_minister_1_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character = POL_Jusef_Pilsudsky } }
				country_event = poland.23
			}
			add_ideas = Jozef_Higersberger add_ideas = Jozef_Higersberger add_ideas = Francis_Pius_Radziwill add_ideas = Vladislav_Studnitsky add_ideas = Eustachy_Sapieha
		}

	option = {
		name = poland.147.a

				former_russian_empire_ukraine_country = yes
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			}
			ROOT = {

					target = PREV
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_array = {
						array = ENG.rcw_supported_states
						value = UKR.id
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = FRA.rcw_supported_states
						value = UKR.id
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = USA.rcw_supported_states
						value = UKR.id
					}
					is_in_array = {
						array = ITA.rcw_supported_states
						value = UKR.id
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = POL_antanta_ne_dovolnya_tt
			random_list = {
				seed = random
				40 = {
					FROM = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = POL modifier = BLR_yhytshenie_otnocheniy } }
				}
				60 = {
				   FROM = { country_event = { id = poland.131 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size > 89999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size > 119999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size > 129999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size > 139999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size > 149999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size > 159999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size > 169999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size > 179999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size > 189999 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.147.b
		add_war_support = -0.03
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = { add = 1 FROM = { has_opinion = { target = POL value > 30 } } }
			modifier = { add = 1 FROM = { has_opinion = { target = POL value > 50 } } }
			modifier = { add = 1 FROM = { has_opinion = { target = POL value > 70 } } }

	id = poland.162 #Восстание польских крестьян
	title = poland.162.t
	desc = poland.162.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_pol_krestyan_vosst
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.162.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialism popularity = -0.2 }
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = POL_seim_radsoc
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_radsoc_yacheiki_1
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_radsoc_yacheiki_2
				has_country_flag = POL_radsoc_sabotash_pra
				has_country_flag = POL_tainy_shron_v_syolah
				has_country_flag = POL_podgotov_k_deistv
				has_country_flag = POL_seim_radsoc_yacheiki
			}
		}
		start_civil_war = {
			ideology = radical_socialism
			size = 0
			capital = 88
			states = { 88 90 1117 92 925 904 }
			keep_political_leader = no
			add_civil_war_target = POL
			division_template = {
				name = "Krestyanskoe opolchenie"
				regiments = {
					militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				}
				is_locked = no
			}

country_event = {
	id = poland.189 #Чехословацкая Республика отказывает
	title = poland.189.t
	desc = poland.189.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_pol_teshin_konflict
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = poland.189.a
		CZE = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = POL modifier = BLR_yhytshenie_otnocheniy } }
		if = {
			limit = { CZE = { NOT = { has_country_flag = POL_cze_yes_pleibescit } } }
			start_border_war = {
				change_state_after_war = yes
				attacker = {
					state = 1467
					num_provinces = 2
					on_win = poland.191
					on_lose = poland.192
				}
				defender = {
					state = 72
					num_provinces = 1
					on_win = poland.191
					on_lose = poland.192
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { CZE = { has_country_flag = POL_cze_yes_pleibescit } }
			start_border_war = {
				change_state_after_war = yes
				attacker = {
					state = 1467
					num_provinces = 2
					on_win = poland.191
					on_lose = poland.192
				}
				defender = {
					state = 72
					num_provinces = 1
					on_win = poland.191
					on_lose = poland.192
				}
			}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = {
					array = ENG.rcw_supported_states
					value = POL.id
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				seed = random
				70 = {
					ENG = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = POL modifier = BLR_yhytshenie_otnocheniy } }
				}
				30 = {
				   ENG = { country_event = { id = poland.131 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = {
					array = FRA.rcw_supported_states
					value = POL.id
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				seed = random
				70 = {
					FRA = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = POL modifier = BLR_yhytshenie_otnocheniy } }
				}
				30 = {
				   FRA = { country_event = { id = poland.131 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}	
		IF = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = {
					array = USA.rcw_supported_states
					value = POL.id
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				seed = random
				70 = {
					USA = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = POL modifier = BLR_yhytshenie_otnocheniy } }
				}
				30 = {
				   USA = { country_event = { id = poland.131 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}	
		IF = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = {
					array = ITA.rcw_supported_states
					value = POL.id
				}
			}
			random_list = {
				seed = random
				70 = {
					ITA = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = POL modifier = BLR_yhytshenie_otnocheniy } }
				}
				30 = {
				   ITA = { country_event = { id = poland.131 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size > 59999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size > 69999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size > 79999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size > 89999 } }
			modifier = { add = 5 has_army_manpower = { size > 99999 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = poland.189.b
		CZE = { add_opinion_modifier = { target = POL modifier = BLR_yhytshenie_otnocheniy } }
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = { add = 5 has_army_manpower = { size < 59999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size < 69999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size < 79999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size < 89999 } }
			modifier = { add = 1 has_army_manpower = { size < 99999 } }
		}
	}

		hidden_effect = { NWA = { set_country_leader_portrait = { ideology = national_syndicalism portrait = GFX_Portrait_Bulak_Balahovich_pol } } }
		every_possible_country = {
			limit = { has_character = BLR_Bulak_Balahovich }
			remove_country_leader_role = { character = BLR_Bulak_Balahovich ideology = national_syndicalism_ideology }
			BLR_Bulak_Balahovich = { set_nationality = ROOT }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			division_template = {
				name = "Kavalerijskaya diviziya Balahovicha"
				regiments = {
					cavalry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					cavalry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				}
				support = {
					recon = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					field_guns = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					logistics_company = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				}
				is_locked = yes
			}
			capital_scope = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Kavalerijskaya diviziya\" division_template = \"Kavalerijskaya diviziya Balahovicha\" start_experience_factor = 0.8 start_equipment_factor = 0.65"
					owner = POL
				} 
			}
		}
		set_portraits = {
			character = BLR_Bulak_Balahovich
			civilian = { large = "GFX_Portrait_Bulak_Balahovich_pol" small = "GFX_Portrait_Bulak_Balahovich_pol_small" }
			army = { large = "GFX_Portrait_Bulak_Balahovich_pol" small = "GFX_Portrait_Bulak_Balahovich_pol_small" }
		}
	}

country_event = {#Балахович идет на контакт с РПК

	}

		days = 3
	}

		custom_effect_tooltip = POL_rpk_recruiting_otryad_balahovich_tt

					AND = {
						has_country_flag = POL_two_ruskya_armya_permkin
						has_country_flag = POL_form_russ_three_army
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = POL_two_ruskya_armya_bred
						has_country_flag = POL_form_army_bredov
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = POL_three_ruskya_armya_balahovich
		}

				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = POL_one_ruskya_armya_permkin
						has_country_flag = POL_form_russ_three_army
					}

						has_country_flag = POL_one_ruskya_armya_bred
						has_country_flag = POL_form_army_bredov
					}
				}
			}

		}
	}

		tag = POL
		OR = {
			NOT = { country_exists = GPU }

			GER = { OR = { controls_state = 86 owns_state = 86 } }
		}
		has_completed_focus = POL_support_velik_pol_vosst
		has_global_flag = POL_war_is_GER

		add_popularity = { ideology = national_syndicalism popularity = 0.03 }
		GER = { country_event = poland.251 }
		GER = { transfer_state = 86 }
	}
}

			LIT = { add_ideas = POL_modifier_sekret_peremirye }
			UKR = { add_ideas = POL_modifier_sekret_peremirye }
			random_country = { 
				limit = { tag = BLR OR = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism } }
				add_ideas = POL_rus_lit_ukr_modifier_sekret_peremirye
			}
			random_country = { 
				limit = { tag = USR OR = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism } }
				add_ideas = POL_rus_lit_ukr_modifier_sekret_peremirye
			}
			random_country = { 
				limit = { tag = LIT OR = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism } }
				add_ideas = POL_rus_lit_ukr_modifier_sekret_peremirye
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { BLR = { OR = { is_in_faction_with = POL is_subject_of = POL } } UKR = { OR = { is_in_faction_with = POL is_subject_of = POL } } }
			RUS = { add_ideas = POL_rus_ukr_blr_modifier_sekret_peremirye }
			UKR = { add_ideas = POL_modifier_sekret_peremirye }
			BLR = { add_ideas = POL_modifier_sekret_peremirye }
			random_country = { 
				limit = { tag = BLR OR = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism } }
				add_ideas = POL_rus_ukr_blr_modifier_sekret_peremirye
			}
			random_country = { 
				limit = { tag = USR OR = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism } }
				add_ideas = POL_rus_ukr_blr_modifier_sekret_peremirye
			}
			random_country = { 
				limit = { tag = LIT OR = { has_government = radical_socialism has_government = communism } }
				add_ideas = POL_rus_ukr_blr_modifier_sekret_peremirye
			}
		}

			OR = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = POL
					AND = { 
						has_global_flag = POL_RUS_litva_neutrality
						has_global_flag = POL_RUS_vilnus_in_poland
						has_global_flag = POL_RUS_litva_annex
					}
				}

					original_tag = RUS
					AND = { 
						has_global_flag = POL_RUS_litva_neutrality
						has_global_flag = POL_RUS_litva_annex
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
	}

		trigger = {
			NOT = {

							has_global_flag = POL_RUS_vilnus_in_poland

country_event = { #Итоги переговоров
	id = poland.273
	title = poland.273.t
	desc = poland.273.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_pol_itogi_peregovor

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	
	option = {
		name = poland.273.a
		add_stability = 0.08
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = POL }
			news_event = { id = news_n.1011 hours = 1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				random_country = { limit = { has_idea = POL_modifier_sekret_peremirye } remove_ideas = POL_modifier_sekret_peremirye }
				random_country = { limit = { has_idea = POL_rus_modifier_sekret_peremirye } remove_ideas = POL_rus_modifier_sekret_peremirye }
				random_country = { limit = { has_idea = POL_rus_ukr_modifier_sekret_peremirye } remove_ideas = POL_rus_ukr_modifier_sekret_peremirye }
				random_country = { limit = { has_idea = POL_rus_blr_modifier_sekret_peremirye } remove_ideas = POL_rus_blr_modifier_sekret_peremirye }
				random_country = { limit = { has_idea = POL_rus_lit_modifier_sekret_peremirye } remove_ideas = POL_rus_lit_modifier_sekret_peremirye }
				random_country = { limit = { has_idea = POL_rus_lit_blr_modifier_sekret_peremirye } remove_ideas = POL_rus_lit_blr_modifier_sekret_peremirye }
				random_country = { limit = { has_idea = POL_rus_lit_ukr_modifier_sekret_peremirye } remove_ideas = POL_rus_lit_ukr_modifier_sekret_peremirye }
				random_country = { limit = { has_idea = POL_rus_ukr_blr_modifier_sekret_peremirye } remove_ideas = POL_rus_ukr_blr_modifier_sekret_peremirye }
			}
			if = { ############################################## Исход нейтральной Литвы
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = POL_RUS_litva_neutrality_itog
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = LIT
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = POL
							is_controlled_by = POL
						}
					}
					LIT = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = LIT
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = RUS
							is_controlled_by = RUS
						}
					}
					LIT = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = { original_tag = BLR OR = { is_subject_of = RUS is_in_faction_with = RUS } }
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = LIT
							OR = {
								is_owned_by = PREV
								is_controlled_by = PREV
							}
						}
						LIT = { transfer_state = PREV }
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = { original_tag = LIT OR = { is_subject_of = RUS is_in_faction_with = RUS } }
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = LIT
							OR = {
								is_owned_by = PREV
								is_controlled_by = PREV
							}
						}
						LIT = { transfer_state = PREV }
					}
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = { original_tag = BLR OR = { is_subject_of = POL is_in_faction_with = POL } }
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = LIT
							OR = {
								is_owned_by = PREV
								is_controlled_by = PREV
							}
						}
						LIT = { transfer_state = PREV }
					}
				}
				LIT = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = { has_government = communism has_government = radical_socialism }
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = conservatism }
					}
					add_ideas = neutral_foreign_policy_law
					POL = { end_puppet = LIT }
					RUS = { end_puppet = LIT }
					leave_faction = yes
					set_truce = {
						target = RUS
						days = 730
					}
					set_truce = {
						target = POL
						days = 730
					}
				}
			}


			if = { ############################################## Исход окуппация Вильнюса
				limit = { has_global_flag = POL_RUS_vilnus_in_poland_itog }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = LIT
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = POL
							is_controlled_by = POL
						}
						NOT = {
							state = 784
							state = 1366
						}
					}
					LIT = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = LIT
						OR = {
							is_owned_by = RUS
							is_controlled_by = RUS
						}
					}
					LIT = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
				random_country = {
					limit = { original_tag = BLR OR = { is_subject_of = RUS is_in_faction_with = RUS } }
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = LIT
							OR = {
								is_owned_by = PREV
								is_controlled_by = PREV
							}
						}
						LIT = { transfer_state = PREV }
					}
				}

					}
				}

			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {

								has_global_flag = POL_RUS_litva_neutrality

					}
				}
			}

		}
	}

		add_war_support = -0.05
		add_stability = -0.05
